template$<$std\+::float\+\_\+round\+\_\+style R$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehalf__float_1_1detail_a239ec58092b4e4849b444baee1a01088}{uint16}} half\+\_\+float\+::detail\+::float2half\+\_\+impl (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float}]{value}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehalf__float_1_1detail_a5e245748a3cc20e348dd92383d99d03c}{true\+\_\+type}}}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert IEEE single-\/precision to half-\/precision. Credit for this goes to \href{ftp://ftp.fox-toolkit.org/pub/fasthalffloatconversion.pdf}{\texttt{Jeroen van der Zijp}}. 
\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em R} & rounding mode to use, {\ttfamily std\+::round\+\_\+indeterminate} for fastest rounding \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{namespacehalf__float_1_1detail_a62e0b5eaa7fb70b52bc00cf87ef3f3ea}\index{half\_float::detail@{half\_float::detail}!half\_cast@{half\_cast}}
\index{half\_cast@{half\_cast}!half\_float::detail@{half\_float::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{half\_cast()}{half\_cast()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacehalf__float_1_1detail_a62e0b5eaa7fb70b52bc00cf87ef3f3ea} 
template$<$typename T, typename U$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{structhalf__float_1_1detail_1_1half__caster}{half\+\_\+caster}}$<$ T, U $>$\+::type half\+\_\+float\+::detail\+::half\+\_\+cast (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{U}]{arg}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Cast to or from half-\/precision floating point number. This casts between \doxylink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half} and any built-\/in arithmetic type. Floating point types are converted via an explicit cast to/from {\ttfamily float} (using the rounding mode of the built-\/in single precision implementation) and thus any possible warnings due to an otherwise implicit conversion to/from {\ttfamily float} will be suppressed. Integer types are converted directly using the given rounding mode, without any roundtrip over {\ttfamily float} that a {\ttfamily static\+\_\+cast} would otherwise do. It uses the default rounding mode.

Using this cast with neither of the two types being a \doxylink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half} or with any of the two types not being a built-\/in arithmetic type (apart from \doxylink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}, of course) results in a compiler error and casting between \doxylink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}s is just a no-\/op. 
\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & destination type (half or built-\/in arithmetic type) \\
\hline
{\em U} & source type (half or built-\/in arithmetic type) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em arg} & value to cast \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\itshape arg} converted to destination type 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{namespacehalf__float_1_1detail_a10a9c9bad301b0c8b2b99371c0f487f3}\index{half\_float::detail@{half\_float::detail}!half\_cast@{half\_cast}}
\index{half\_cast@{half\_cast}!half\_float::detail@{half\_float::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{half\_cast()}{half\_cast()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacehalf__float_1_1detail_a10a9c9bad301b0c8b2b99371c0f487f3} 
template$<$typename T, std\+::float\+\_\+round\+\_\+style R, typename U$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{structhalf__float_1_1detail_1_1half__caster}{half\+\_\+caster}}$<$ T, U, R $>$\+::type half\+\_\+float\+::detail\+::half\+\_\+cast (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{U}]{arg}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Cast to or from half-\/precision floating point number. This casts between \doxylink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half} and any built-\/in arithmetic type. Floating point types are converted via an explicit cast to/from {\ttfamily float} (using the rounding mode of the built-\/in single precision implementation) and thus any possible warnings due to an otherwise implicit conversion to/from {\ttfamily float} will be suppressed. Integer types are converted directly using the given rounding mode, without any roundtrip over {\ttfamily float} that a {\ttfamily static\+\_\+cast} would otherwise do.

Using this cast with neither of the two types being a \doxylink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half} or with any of the two types not being a built-\/in arithmetic type (apart from \doxylink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}, of course) results in a compiler error and casting between \doxylink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}s is just a no-\/op. 
\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & destination type (half or built-\/in arithmetic type) \\
\hline
{\em R} & rounding mode to use. \\
\hline
{\em U} & source type (half or built-\/in arithmetic type) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em arg} & value to cast \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\itshape arg} converted to destination type 
\end{DoxyReturn}
